31 typedef struct {
32  int field_type, /* either NID_X9_62_prime_field or
33  * NID_X9_62_characteristic_two_field */
34  seed_len, param_len;
35  unsigned int cofactor; /* promoted to BN_ULONG */
36 } EC_CURVE_DATA;
37

2980 static EC_GROUP *ec_group_new_from_data(const ec_list_element curve)
2981 {
2982  EC_GROUP *group = NULL;
2983  EC_POINT *P = NULL;
2984  BN_CTX *ctx = NULL;
2985  BIGNUM *p = NULL, *a = NULL, *b = NULL, *x = NULL, *y = NULL, *order =
2986  NULL;
2987  int ok = 0;
2988  int seed_len, param_len;
2989  const EC_METHOD *meth;
2990  const EC_CURVE_DATA *data;
2991  const unsigned char *params;
2992 
2993  /* If no curve data curve method must handle everything */
2994  if (curve.data == NULL)
2995  return EC_GROUP_new(curve.meth != NULL ? curve.meth() : NULL);
2996 
2997  if ((ctx = BN_CTX_new()) == NULL) {
2998  ECerr(EC_F_EC_GROUP_NEW_FROM_DATA, ERR_R_MALLOC_FAILURE);
2999  goto err;
3000  }
3001 
3002  data = curve.data;
3003  seed_len = data->seed_len;
3004  param_len = data->param_len;
3005  params = (const unsigned char *)(data + 1); /* skip header */
3006  params += seed_len; /* skip seed */
3007 
3008  if ((p = BN_bin2bn(params + 0 * param_len, param_len, NULL)) == NULL
3009  || (a = BN_bin2bn(params + 1 * param_len, param_len, NULL)) == NULL
3010  || (b = BN_bin2bn(params + 2 * param_len, param_len, NULL)) == NULL) {
3011  ECerr(EC_F_EC_GROUP_NEW_FROM_DATA, ERR_R_BN_LIB);
3012  goto err;
3013  }
3014 
3015  if (curve.meth != 0) {
3016  meth = curve.meth();
3017  if (((group = EC_GROUP_new(meth)) == NULL) ||
3018  (!(group->meth->group_set_curve(group, p, a, b, ctx)))) {
3019  ECerr(EC_F_EC_GROUP_NEW_FROM_DATA, ERR_R_EC_LIB);
3020  goto err;
3021  }
3022  } else if (data->field_type == NID_X9_62_prime_field) {
3023  if ((group = EC_GROUP_new_curve_GFp(p, a, b, ctx)) == NULL) {
3024  ECerr(EC_F_EC_GROUP_NEW_FROM_DATA, ERR_R_EC_LIB);
3025  goto err;
3026  }
3027  }
3028 #ifndef OPENSSL_NO_EC2M
3029  else { /* field_type ==
3030  * NID_X9_62_characteristic_two_field */
3031 
3032  if ((group = EC_GROUP_new_curve_GF2m(p, a, b, ctx)) == NULL) {
3033  ECerr(EC_F_EC_GROUP_NEW_FROM_DATA, ERR_R_EC_LIB);
3034  goto err;
3035  }
3036  }
3037 #endif
3038 
3039  if ((P = EC_POINT_new(group)) == NULL) {
3040  ECerr(EC_F_EC_GROUP_NEW_FROM_DATA, ERR_R_EC_LIB);
3041  goto err;
3042  }
3043 
3044  if ((x = BN_bin2bn(params + 3 * param_len, param_len, NULL)) == NULL
3045  || (y = BN_bin2bn(params + 4 * param_len, param_len, NULL)) == NULL) {
3046  ECerr(EC_F_EC_GROUP_NEW_FROM_DATA, ERR_R_BN_LIB);
3047  goto err;
3048  }
3049  if (!EC_POINT_set_affine_coordinates_GFp(group, P, x, y, ctx)) {
3050  ECerr(EC_F_EC_GROUP_NEW_FROM_DATA, ERR_R_EC_LIB);
3051  goto err;
3052  }
3053  if ((order = BN_bin2bn(params + 5 * param_len, param_len, NULL)) == NULL
3054  || !BN_set_word(x, (BN_ULONG)data->cofactor)) {
3055  ECerr(EC_F_EC_GROUP_NEW_FROM_DATA, ERR_R_BN_LIB);
3056  goto err;
3057  }
3058  if (!EC_GROUP_set_generator(group, P, order, x)) {
3059  ECerr(EC_F_EC_GROUP_NEW_FROM_DATA, ERR_R_EC_LIB);
3060  goto err;
3061  }
3062  if (seed_len) {
3063  if (!EC_GROUP_set_seed(group, params - seed_len, seed_len)) {
3064  ECerr(EC_F_EC_GROUP_NEW_FROM_DATA, ERR_R_EC_LIB);
3065  goto err;
3066  }
3067  }
3068  ok = 1;
3069  err:
3070  if (!ok) {
3071  EC_GROUP_free(group);
3072  group = NULL;
3073  }
3074  EC_POINT_free(P);
3075  BN_CTX_free(ctx);
3076  BN_free(p);
3077  BN_free(a);
3078  BN_free(b);
3079  BN_free(order);
3080  BN_free(x);
3081  BN_free(y);
3082  return group;
3083 }
3084 
3085 EC_GROUP *EC_GROUP_new_by_curve_name(int nid)
3086 {
3087  size_t i;
3088  EC_GROUP *ret = NULL;
3089 
3090  if (nid <= 0)
3091  return NULL;
3092 
3093  for (i = 0; i < curve_list_length; i++)
3094  if (curve_list[i].nid == nid) {
3095  ret = ec_group_new_from_data(curve_list[i]);
3096  break;
3097  }
3098 
3099  if (ret == NULL) {
3100  ECerr(EC_F_EC_GROUP_NEW_BY_CURVE_NAME, EC_R_UNKNOWN_GROUP);
3101  return NULL;
3102  }
3103 
3104  EC_GROUP_set_curve_name(ret, nid);
3105 
3106  return ret;
3107 }
3108 
3109 size_t EC_get_builtin_curves(EC_builtin_curve *r, size_t nitems)
3110 {
3111  size_t i, min;
3112 
3113  if (r == NULL || nitems == 0)
3114  return curve_list_length;
3115 
3116  min = nitems < curve_list_length ? nitems : curve_list_length;
3117 
3118  for (i = 0; i < min; i++) {
3119  r[i].nid = curve_list[i].nid;
3120  r[i].comment = curve_list[i].comment;
3121  }
3122 
3123  return curve_list_length;
3124 }

3151 const char *EC_curve_nid2nist(int nid)
3152 {
3153  size_t i;
3154  for (i = 0; i < OSSL_NELEM(nist_curves); i++) {
3155  if (nist_curves[i].nid == nid)
3156  return nist_curves[i].name;
3157  }
3158  return NULL;
3159 }
3160 
3161 int EC_curve_nist2nid(const char *name)
3162 {
3163  size_t i;
3164  for (i = 0; i < OSSL_NELEM(nist_curves); i++) {
3165  if (strcmp(nist_curves[i].name, name) == 0)
3166  return nist_curves[i].nid;
3167  }
3168  return NID_undef;
3169 }
